21 trait IntEncodersImplicits extends Serializable {
22 
23   // RuleResultWithProcessor's are lost in serialization by design, they only make sense in a given run
24 
25   /**
26    * Converts the DQ results to and from Int and RuleResult's.  Probability is processed by the value / PassedInt
27    */
28   implicit val ruleResultToInt: Injection[RuleResult, Int] = Injection(
29     {
30       case r: RuleResult => Serializing.ruleResultToInt(r)
31     },
32     {
33       case SoftFailedInt => SoftFailed
34       case DisabledRuleInt => DisabledRule
35       case FailedInt => Failed
36       case PassedInt => Passed
37       case a: Int => Probability(a.toDouble / PassedInt)
38     })
39 
40 }
41 
42 object IntEncoders extends IntEncodersImplicits {
43 }
44 
45 trait IdEncodersImplicits extends Serializable {
46   implicit val versionedIdNotNullable = new NotCatalystNullable[VersionedId] {}
47 
48   // try just id first
49   implicit val versionedIdTo: Injection[VersionedId, Long] = Injection(
50     {
51       case Id(id, version) => ((id.toLong) << 32) | (version & 0xffffffffL)
52     },
53     {
54       case a: Long =>
55         PackId.unpack(a)
56     })
57 }
58 
59 object IdEncoders extends IdEncodersImplicits {
60 
61 }

159 object EmptyMap extends MapData {
160   override val keyArray: ArrayData = new org.apache.spark.sql.catalyst.util.GenericArrayData(Array.empty)
161   override val valueArray: ArrayData = new org.apache.spark.sql.catalyst.util.GenericArrayData(Array.empty)
162   override def numElements(): Int = 0
163 
164   override def copy(): MapData = this
165 
166   override def toString: String = {
167     s"keys: $keyArray, values: $valueArray"
168   }
169 }
170 
171 object MapUtils {
172   def toScalaMap(map: MapData, keyType: DataType, valueType: DataType): Map[Any, Any] = {
173     val keys = map.keyArray.toObjectArray(keyType)
174     val values = map.valueArray.toObjectArray(valueType)
175     keys.zip(values).toMap
176   }
177 
178   /**
179    * Assuming MapData entries are stable, as they are array backed, over a dataset.  When the position of 'what' is not in the cachedPositions a full search is performed with the new location being returned in addition.
180    *
181    * @param mapData the source mapdata to search through.
182    * @param cachedPositions already known positions to check for what
183    * @param what compared against the keyArray to obtain the position
184    * @param getValue obtain the value from the mapData, with any necessary conversions, against the index parameter
185    * @tparam T
186    * @return (result from getValue or null when not found, either cachedPositions or cachedPositions and a newly found position)
187    */
188   def getMapEntry[T <: AnyRef](mapData: MapData, cachedPositions: Seq[Int], what: Any)(getValue: Int => T): (T, Seq[Int]) = {
189     val keys = mapData.keyArray()
190     val n = keys.numElements()
191     val acc = (idx: Int) => keys.getLong(idx)
192 
193     def search() = {
194       var i = 0
195       var found = false
196       while (i < n && !found) {
197         if (acc(i) == what) {
198           found = true
199         } else {
200           i += 1
201         }
202       }
203       if (!found)
204         -1
205       else
206         i
207     }
208 
209     def withCached() =
210       cachedPositions.find { i =>
211         if (i < n)
212           acc(i) == what
213         else
214           false
215       }
216 
217     withCached().map(i => (getValue(i), cachedPositions))
218       .getOrElse {
219         val r = search()
220         if (r == -1)
221           (null.asInstanceOf[T], cachedPositions)
222         else
223           (getValue(r), cachedPositions :+ r)
224       }
225   }
226 
227 }
